Dr. Downie uses the latest technology tools and treatment techniques when treating her patients to ensure that they only receive the best care. Furthermore she has years of experience practicing dermatology and is highly trained in providing a range of dermatology procedures and treatments.Among some of the dermatology services that Dr. Downie offers are Botox injections Chemical Peels Exilis Fraxel Restore Juvederm Laser Hair Removal Restylane Silk Perlane Radiesse Sculptra Sclerotherapy Skin Cancer Surgery Patch Testing as well as Kybella Vanquish Fat Melting. 

To start her higher education Dr. Downie attended the Tufts University and graduated with her Bachelor of Science degree in Biology and Psychology.She then attended the American University and graduated with her Master of Arts degree in Biology. Dr. Downie followed this by earning her Doctor of Medicine degree by attending the SUNY-Health Science Center located in Brooklyn. After this she completed pediatric residency which lasted for two years at the New York Hospital-Cornell Medical Center. Dr. Downie then completed her residency in dermatology by going to the Mount Sinai Medical Center located in New York. 

She has professional affiliations with a number of well-known and esteemed medical societies and organizations including the American Academy of Dermatology the Skin Cancer the Women’s Dermatologic Society as well as the American Society for Dermatologic Surgery.

<br>ContactDescription----Eric Zinczenko was named Chief Executive Officer of Bonnier Corp. in June 2015. Prior to that he served as Executive Vice President.

Eric joined Bonnier Corp. from Time Inc. in 2007 as part of Bonnier’s original management team. Prior to his promotion to Executive Vice President Eric led one of the company’s largest business units the Bonnier Men’s Group which includes three of the country’s largest special-interest titles Popular Science Field & Stream and Outdoor Life. Eric was responsible for expanding the brands into a multichannel media group with licensing events TV and film. He’s credited with signing a number of highly profitable partnerships for his brands and in 2011 he helped the company acquire Hearst’s Cycle World.

Prior to joining Bonnier Corp. Eric had successful sales-management positions with Outside The New Yorker Bicycling and Scuba Diving. Eric started his career at Rodale becoming ad director of Bicycling at age 26. In 2008 Eric was inducted into MIN’s Sales Executive of the Year Hall of Fame for his contributions to and success in publishing.

Eric’s interests are many — 600 sky dives and 1000 scuba dives including more than 400 dives in underwater caves in North America. He has also run multiple ironman and triathlon events.

<br>ContactDescription----Elizabeth Burnham Murphy was appointed Bonnier Corp.’s first Chief Marketing Officer on the corporate level in December 2013.

Liz has created new revenue opportunities for Bonnier Corp. brands through media extensions such as full-length television series and licensing opportunities which include the launch of the Outdoor Life apparel line in Sears stores across the country. In 2013 she instituted a new corporate unit Bonnier Corp. Custom Solutions which supports the creation of custom content products and services for Bonnier Corp.’s clients and partners.

Liz has two young children and shares many Bonnier Corp. passions. An avid angler shooter and amateur photographer her favorite pursuits are connected to the outdoors and spending free time with family in New York’s Adirondack Mountains.

<br>ContactDescription----Sean is a 20-year industry veteran who has consistently delivered revenue growth to organizations he has been a part of. Sean joined Bonnier in 2011 as Chief Brand Development Officer responsible for the business and brand development of the company’s 30-plus brands and the growth of new revenue streams. His other duties included programmatic advertising the digital distribution of video and editorial content and consumer products. As Chief Digital Revenue Officer Sean is charged with managing Bonnier’s brand sellers to achieve increased premium sell-through of digital inventory and higher CPMs in addition to his previous responsibilities.
 
Prior to joining Bonnier Sean served as President Enterprises Division for Source Interlink Media. He joined them in 2000 as Senior Director Licensing Sales for Primedia (purchased by Source Interlink) where he oversaw sales for an extensive portfolio of automotive and outdoor brands. Sean next served as Vice President of Primedia Enterprises the company’s business development arm from 2002 to 2004 and Senior Vice President of Sales Marketing and Retail Development from 2004 to 2006. In this position he secured licensing deals and forged creative partnerships retail programs and new content plays for popular enthusiast brands such as Surfer Hot Rod and Motor Trend.
 
Sean began his career in sales and marketing with management positions at WindChaser Products Inc. and sales at Paramount Pictures Domestic Television Distribution. He lives in Los Angeles California with his family.

<br>ContactDescription----Territory: Southern California from San Luis Obispo to San Diego Nevada Utah Arizona and New Mexico.Gary Newkirk’s introduction to the bicycle industry was in the 1970’s when his family bought a family shop in Anaheim. While in college at the University of California San Diego and later at UCLA Gary managed the bicycle co-op at UCSD and worked at Bikeology while finishing his degree at UCLA. Following a brief diversion into the finance world after college he found his way back to the industry with stints at Two Wheel Transit Authority West Coast Cycles and Blackburn Designs. Sports photography was always a passion and while at Blackburn he began shooting events for Winning Magazine and its sister publication Triathlete Magazine. A desire to broaden his sports coverage led to a staff photographer position at Allsport Photography (now Getty Images). While at Allsport he began specializing in golf photography leading to a position with Golf World / Golf Digest. After covering more than 500 professional golf tournaments he found himself drawn back at his first love cycling. Gary joined Bicycle Retailer and Industry News in September 2011 as the Director of Sales and Marketing.
